the	/ðə/	det.; art.	这；那（定冠词）	the same;the first;the more	The book on the table is mine.	桌上的那本书是我的。			元音前常读 /ðiː/，辅音前读 /ðə/。	A1	1
be	/biː/	verb	是；在；成为	be careful;be honest;there be	She wants to be a doctor one day.	她希望有一天成为医生。	exist;remain		am/is/are/was/were 都是 be 的词形。	A1	2
and	/ænd/	conj.	和；并且	and so on;bread and butter;and then	Tom and Lily walked home together.	汤姆和莉莉一起走回家。	plus;also	but;or	连接对等成分，可记成“一加一”。	A1	3
of	/əv/	prep.	……的；属于	a lot of;kind of;proud of	This is a photo of my family.	这是我家的一张照片。	from;about		弱读常见 /əv/，别总读成 /ɒv/。	A1	4
to	/tuː/	prep.; particle	到；向；去；不定式标记	go to;listen to;want to	I need to finish my homework tonight.	我今晚需要完成作业。	towards;for	from	作不定式时多弱读 /tə/。	A1	5
a	/ə/	det.; art.	一个（不定冠词）	a bit;a few;have a look	She bought a gift for her friend.	她给朋友买了一份礼物。	one;any	the	辅音前用 a，元音前改用 an。	A1	6
in	/ɪn/	prep.; adv.	在……里；在……时	in time;in fact;in the morning	There are three books in the bag.	包里有三本书。	inside;within	out;outside	in 像走进门里。	A1	7
have	/hæv/	verb	有；吃；经历；助动词	have lunch;have to;have fun	They have a small flat near the station.	他们在车站附近有一套小公寓。	own;possess	lack	完成时里 have/has + 过去分词。	A1	8
it	/ɪt/	pron.	它；这；形式主语	it seems;find it;make it	It is raining hard this afternoon.	今天下午雨下得很大。	this;that		指物、动物、时间天气常用 it。	A1	9
you	/juː/	pron.	你；你们	thank you;see you;you know	Can you help me with this box?	你能帮我搬这个箱子吗？	one;people		单复数同形，语气看语境。	A1	10
he	/hiː/	pron.	他	he says;he is;there he is	He is waiting for the bus outside.	他在外面等公交车。		she	主格 he，宾格 him，所有格 his。	A1	11
for	/fɔː(r)/	prep.; conj.	为了；给；因为；达……之久	for example;look for;wait for	This gift is for your sister.	这份礼物是给你妹妹的。	because of;during	against	表目的、对象或时间长度都很常见。	A1	12
they	/ðeɪ/	pron.	他们；她们；它们	they say;there they are;as they	They arrived early for the meeting.	他们早早到了会议现场。	people		主格 they，宾格 them，所有格 their。	A1	13
not	/nɒt/	adv.; particle	不；没有	not only;do not;not yet	I do not want to go out tonight.	我今晚不想出门。	no;never	yes	常缩成 n't，如 don't / isn't。	A1	14
that	/ðæt/	det.; pron.; conj.; adv.	那个；那；引导从句	so that;that day;find that	I think that the answer is correct.	我认为这个答案是正确的。	which;this	this	可指物，也可引导 that 从句。	A1	15
we	/wiː/	pron.	我们	we are;as we;shall we	We are planning a trip next month.	我们计划下个月去旅行。	us		主格 we，宾格 us，所有格 our。	A1	16
on	/ɒn/	prep.; adv.	在……上；关于；继续	on time;on the table;turn on	The keys are on the kitchen table.	钥匙在厨房桌上。	upon;about	off;under	接触表面用 on，反义常想 off。	A1	17
with	/wɪð/	prep.	和……一起；用；带有	with care;deal with;along with	She went to the cinema with her friends.	她和朋友们一起去看电影了。	alongside;using	without	with 的反义是 without。	A1	18
this	/ðɪs/	det.; pron.; adv.	这；这个	this morning;this way;like this	This café makes excellent coffee.	这家咖啡馆咖啡很好。	these;that	that	近处 this，远处 that；复数 these。	A1	19
i	/aɪ/	pron.	我	I think;I am;I hope	I usually get up at seven.	我通常七点起床。	me		句子开头须大写 I。	A1	20
do	/duː/	verb; aux.	做；干；助动词	do homework;do well;how do you	What do you usually do at weekends?	你周末通常做什么？	perform;act		疑问/否定句里常用 do/does/did。	A1	21
as	/æz/	prep.; conj.; adv.	作为；当……时；像；因为	as well;as soon as;as for	She works as a nurse in hospital.	她在医院当护士。	like;while		as…as 表示同等比较。	A1	22
at	/æt/	prep.	在（地点/时间点）；朝向	at home;at least;look at	We will meet at the station at six.	我们六点在车站见面。	in;on		具体时刻、较小地点常用 at。	A1	23
she	/ʃiː/	pron.	她	she says;she is;there she is	She teaches English at our school.	她在我们学校教英语。		he	主格 she，宾格 her，所有格 her。	A1	24
but	/bʌt/	conj.; prep.; adv.	但是；除了	but also;nothing but;last but not least	I like tea, but I prefer coffee.	我喜欢茶，但更爱咖啡。	however;yet	and	转折用 but，语气比 however 更口语。	A1	25
from	/frɒm/	prep.	从；来自；由于	from home;far from;different from	This letter is from my uncle in London.	这封信来自我在伦敦的叔叔。	out of;since	to;towards	from A to B：从 A 到 B。	A1	26
by	/baɪ/	prep.; adv.	被；通过；在旁边；到……之前	by bus;by chance;by the way	The report was written by my colleague.	这份报告是我同事写的。	via;near		被动语态里 by 引出动作执行者。	A1	27
will	/wɪl/	modal; noun	将；会；意愿；遗嘱	will be;free will;if you will	They will call you tomorrow morning.	他们明天早上会给你打电话。	shall;going to	won't	表将来也表意愿；won't = will not。	A1	28
or	/ɔː(r)/	conj.	或者；否则	or so;either or;or else	Would you like tea or coffee?	你想喝茶还是咖啡？	alternatively	and	either…or… 表示二选一。	A1	29
say	/seɪ/	verb	说；表示	say hello;say sorry;that is to say	Please say your name clearly.	请清楚地说出你的名字。	speak;tell;state	listen	say 侧重说的内容；tell 常带对象。	A1	30
go	/ɡəʊ/	verb	去；走；变得	go home;go on;go shopping	We usually go to school by bike.	我们通常骑自行车去上学。	leave;travel;move	stay;come	go + -ing：go swimming / go shopping。	A1	31
so	/səʊ/	adv.; conj.	如此；所以；这样	so that;so far;and so on	It was raining, so we stayed inside.	下雨了，所以我们待在屋里。	therefore;very		既表程度（so tired），也表结果。	A1	32
all	/ɔːl/	det.; pron.; adv.	全部；所有；完全	all day;above all;all over	All students must wear school uniforms.	所有学生都必须穿校服。	every;entire	none;some	all of us = 我们全部。	A1	33
if	/ɪf/	conj.	如果；是否	if possible;what if;as if	If it rains, we will cancel the trip.	如果下雨，我们就取消这次旅行。	whether;when		真实条件用 will；虚拟则改时态。	A1	34
one	/wʌn/	num.; pron.; det.	一；一个人；某一个	one day;one of;the one	One of my friends lives abroad.	我的一个朋友住在国外。	a;single	many;none	可替代前文名词：this one / that one。	A1	35
would	/wʊd/	modal	会；愿意；过去将来	would like;would rather;would you	I would like a glass of water, please.	请给我一杯水。	could;might		would like = want 的更礼貌说法。	A1	36
about	/əˈbaʊt/	prep.; adv.	关于；大约；到处	talk about;about time;think about	We talked about our weekend plans after lunch.	午饭后我们聊了周末的计划。	regarding;around	exactly	about 可记成绕着一件事转。	A1	37
can	/kæn/	modal; noun	能；可以；罐头	can do;as you can;can of	Can you open the window, please?	请你把窗户打开好吗？	could;may;able to	cannot	否定 can't；过去/委婉用 could。	A1	38
which	/wɪtʃ/	pron.; det.	哪一个；……的（关系代词）	which one;in which;of which	Which colour do you prefer?	你更喜欢哪种颜色？	that;what		问选择用 which；非限定从句也常用。	A1	39
there	/ðeə(r)/	adv.; pron.	在那里；有（there be）	over there;there is;out there	There is a park near my house.	我家附近有一座公园。	here	here	there be 表“存在”，非地点时也可用。	A1	40
know	/nəʊ/	verb	知道；认识；了解	know about;get to know;as you know	Do you know the way to the museum?	你知道去博物馆怎么走吗？	understand;recognise	ignore	know that… = 知道某事属实。	A1	41
more	/mɔː(r)/	det.; adv.; pron.	更多；更加	more than;once more;more or less	I need more time to finish this task.	我需要更多时间完成这项任务。	additional;extra	less;fewer	比较级：more + 多音节形容词。	A1	42
get	/ɡet/	verb	得到；变得；到达	get up;get ready;get to	How do I get to the railway station?	我怎么去火车站？	receive;become;arrive	lose;give	短语很多：get on / get off / get over。	A1	43
who	/huː/	pron.	谁；……的人	who is;those who;who else	Who left this bag on the chair?	谁把包落在椅子上了？	whom;that		主格 who，宾格正式场合用 whom。	A1	44
like	/laɪk/	prep.; verb; conj.	像；喜欢；例如	like this;feel like;would like	She looks like her mother.	她长得像她母亲。	enjoy;similar to	dislike;unlike	作介词表“像”，作动词表“喜欢”。	A1	45
when	/wen/	adv.; conj.; pron.	什么时候；当……时	when to;by when;since when	When does the train arrive?	火车什么时候到？	while;whenever		既问时间，也引导时间从句。	A1	46
think	/θɪŋk/	verb	想；认为；思索	think about;think of;I think	I think we should leave early.	我认为我们该早点出发。	believe;consider		think of=想起；think about=考虑。	A1	47
make	/meɪk/	verb	做；制造；使	make sure;make a decision;make friends	She made a cake for the party.	她为派对做了一个蛋糕。	create;produce;cause	destroy;break	make sb do = 让某人做某事。	A1	48
time	/taɪm/	noun; verb	时间；次数；时机	on time;take time;have time	We do not have much time left.	我们剩下的时间不多了。	moment;occasion;period		times 可表倍数或次数。	A1	49
see	/siː/	verb	看见；理解；见面	see you;see as;I see	Did you see the notice on the board?	你看到黑板上的通知了吗？	watch;notice;understand	miss;ignore	see 无意识看见；watch 有意观看。	A1	50
what	/wɒt/	pron.; det.; adv.	什么；多么	what about;what if;what for	What is your favourite subject?	你最喜欢的科目是什么？	which;how		What a day! 感叹句很常见。	A1	51
up	/ʌp/	adv.; prep.; adj.	向上；起来；完成	get up;wake up;give up	Please stand up when the teacher comes in.	老师进来时请起立。	upwards;aloft	down	大量动词短语含 up，表完成或上升。	A1	52
some	/sʌm/	det.; pron.; adv.	一些；某个；大约	some people;some of;for some time	Would you like some tea?	你想喝点茶吗？	a few;several	none;all	肯定句多用 some，疑问/否定常改 any。	A1	53
other	/ˈʌðə(r)/	adj.; pron.	其他的；另一个	each other;the other;other than	Do you have any other questions?	你还有其他问题吗？	another;different	same	the other=两者中另一个；others=其他人/物。	A1	54
out	/aʊt/	adv.; prep.; adj.	出去；外面；熄灭	go out;find out;out of	She went out for a short walk.	她出去散了一会儿步。	outside;away	in;inside	out of = 从……出来 / 用完。	A1	55
good	/ɡʊd/	adj.; noun	好的；擅长的；好处	good at;good news;for good	This is a good place for a picnic.	这是一个野餐的好地方。	nice;fine;excellent	bad;poor	better / best 是其比较级与最高级。	A1	56
people	/ˈpiːpl/	noun	人；人们；民族	young people;many people;local people	Many people use public transport every day.	许多人每天使用公共交通。	persons;folks		通常当复数：people are…。	A1	57
year	/jɪə(r)/	noun	年；岁；学年	next year;every year;for years	She spent a year studying abroad.	她在国外学习了一年。	annum;twelve months		years old 表示年龄。	A1	58
take	/teɪk/	verb	拿；带；花费；乘坐	take care;take place;take part	It takes twenty minutes to walk there.	步行到那里要二十分钟。	bring;carry;accept	give;leave	take 强调带走；bring 强调带来。	A1	59
no	/nəʊ/	det.; adv.; interj.	没有；不；不是的	no longer;no one;no problem	There is no milk left in the fridge.	冰箱里没有牛奶了。	not any;none	yes;some	no + 名词 = not any + 名词。	A1	60
well	/wel/	adv.; adj.; interj.	好地；健康的；嗯	as well;well done;get well	She speaks English very well.	她英语说得很好。	fine;properly	badly;ill	作形容词常指健康：feel well。	A1	61
because	/bɪˈkɒz/	conj.	因为	because of;just because;because why	We stayed indoors because it was cold.	因为天冷，我们待在室内。	since;as;for	although	because of + 名词短语。	A1	62
very	/ˈveri/	adv.	非常；很	very much;very good;very well	The film was very interesting.	这部电影非常有趣。	extremely;really	slightly	very + 形容词/副词，不可直接修饰动词。	A1	63
just	/dʒʌst/	adv.; adj.	刚刚；只是；公正的	just now;just in time;just as	I have just finished my homework.	我刚刚做完作业。	only;recently;fair	unfair	完成时里 just 表“刚刚”。	A1	64
come	/kʌm/	verb	来；到达；出现	come back;come from;come on	Please come to my office after class.	下课后请到我办公室来。	arrive;approach	go;leave	come 朝说话者来；go 离开说话者。	A1	65
could	/kʊd/	modal	能；可以；可能（过去或委婉）	could you;could be;as could	Could you open the door for me?	你能帮我开一下门吗？	can;might;would		比 can 更礼貌，也表过去能力。	A1	66
work	/wɜːk/	noun; verb	工作；劳动；起作用	at work;work hard;go to work	She started work at nine this morning.	她今天早上九点开始工作。	job;labour;function	rest;play	不可数常指劳动；job 多指具体职位。	A1	67
use	/juːz/; /juːs/	verb; noun	使用；用途	use up;make use of;in use	May I use your phone for a minute?	我可以用一下你的手机吗？	employ;utilise	waste;ignore	动词读 /juːz/，名词读 /juːs/。	A1	68
than	/ðæn/	conj.; prep.	比	more than;rather than;other than	This book is longer than that one.	这本书比那本更长。	compared with		比较级后接 than。	A1	69
now	/naʊ/	adv.; conj.; noun	现在；目前	right now;from now on;by now	We need to leave now or we will be late.	我们现在就得走，否则会迟到。	currently;at present	then;later	now and then = 偶尔。	A1	70
then	/ðen/	adv.	然后；那时；那么	and then;since then;by then	First wash the vegetables, then cook them.	先洗菜，然后烹调。	next;afterwards;at that time	now	既表顺序，也表“那时”。	A1	71
also	/ˈɔːlsəʊ/	adv.	也；而且	not only also;and also;also known as	She can also speak a little French.	她也会说一点法语。	too;as well;moreover		also 多在句中；too 常在句末。	A1	72
into	/ˈɪntuː/	prep.	进入；变成	go into;turn into;look into	He walked into the classroom quietly.	他安静地走进教室。	inside;in	out of	强调进入内部：into the room。	A1	73
only	/ˈəʊnli/	adv.; adj.	仅仅；唯一的	not only;only if;the only	Only three people came to the meeting.	只有三个人来开会。	just;sole;merely		位置不同可能改变句子重点。	A1	74
look	/lʊk/	verb; noun	看；看起来；外观	look at;look for;look after	Please look at the board carefully.	请仔细看黑板。	see;watch;appear		look at/for/after 搭配义差很大。	A1	75
want	/wɒnt/	verb; noun	想要；需要	want to;want for;in want of	I want to learn how to cook.	我想学做饭。	wish;desire;need	reject	want sb to do = 想让某人做。	A1	76
give	/ɡɪv/	verb	给；提供；产生	give up;give back;give a talk	Could you give me some advice?	你能给我一些建议吗？	offer;provide;hand	take;receive	give sb sth 或 give sth to sb。	A1	77
first	/fɜːst/	det.; adv.; noun	第一；首先；初次	first of all;at first;first time	First, we need to check the timetable.	首先，我们需要核对时刻表。	initial;primary	last;final	at first=起初；first of all=首先。	A1	78
new	/njuː/	adj.	新的；陌生的	new year;brand new;new to	They moved into a new flat last week.	他们上周搬进了新公寓。	fresh;modern;recent	old;used	new to sth = 对……不熟悉。	A1	79
way	/weɪ/	noun; adv.	方式；路；方法	by the way;on the way;in this way	Is this the way to the post office?	这是去邮局的路吗？	method;road;manner		way 既指路，也指做事方法。	A1	80
find	/faɪnd/	verb	找到；发现；觉得	find out;find it hard;find a way	I cannot find my keys anywhere.	我到处都找不到钥匙。	discover;locate;feel	lose;miss	find out = 查明事实。	A1	81
over	/ˈəʊvə(r)/	prep.; adv.; adj.	在……上方；结束；越过	over there;all over;get over	The meeting will be over by five.	会议五点前会结束。	above;across;finished	under	be over = 结束；get over = 克服。	A1	82
any	/ˈeni/	det.; pron.; adv.	任何；一些（疑/否）	any more;in any case;any time	Do you have any questions about the text?	你对课文有任何问题吗？	some;every	none	疑问否定用 any；肯定常用 some。	A1	83
after	/ˈɑːftə(r)/	prep.; conj.; adv.	在……之后	after all;look after;after school	We went for a walk after dinner.	晚饭后我们去散步了。	following;later	before	after all = 毕竟。	A1	84
day	/deɪ/	noun	天；白天；日子	one day;every day;the other day	What a beautiful day it is today!	今天天气真好！	date;daytime	night	day by day = 一天天。	A1	85
where	/weə(r)/	adv.; conj.; pron.	在哪里；……的地方	where to;anywhere;where from	Where did you put the tickets?	你把票放哪里了？	wherever		既问地点，也引导地点从句。	A1	86
thing	/θɪŋ/	noun	东西；事情；情况	for one thing;the thing is;among other things	I have many things to do this weekend.	这个周末我有很多事要做。	matter;object;stuff		口语里 thing 常泛指事情。	A1	87
most	/məʊst/	det.; pron.; adv.	大多数；最	most of;at most;most importantly	Most students in this class like sports.	这个班大多数学生喜欢运动。	majority;nearly all	least;fewest	the most + 形容词 = 最高级。	A1	88
should	/ʃʊd/	modal	应该；理应	should be;should have;why should	You should drink more water every day.	你应该每天多喝水。	ought to;must	shouldn't	should have done = 本该做却未做。	A1	89
need	/niːd/	verb; modal; noun	需要；必要	need to;in need;need for	We need more chairs for the meeting.	我们开会需要更多椅子。	require;want;must		实义动词 need to do；情态否定 needn't。	A1	90
much	/mʌtʃ/	det.; pron.; adv.	许多（不可数）；很	how much;too much;as much as	There is not much sugar left.	剩下的糖不多了。	a lot;greatly	little	much 修不可数；many 修可数。	A1	91
right	/raɪt/	adj.; adv.; noun	正确的；右边；权利	all right;right now;the right to	Turn right at the next traffic lights.	在下一个红绿灯处右转。	correct;proper	wrong;left	既表对错，也表左右与权利。	A1	92
how	/haʊ/	adv.; conj.	如何；怎样；多么	how to;how about;how long	How can I improve my listening skills?	我怎样才能提高听力？	in what way		how + adj./adv. 可表感叹。	A1	93
